On School Physical Education (1) by Lu Xiangqian

It has been several decades since we advocated for new education in our country. What has been the effect? Those with knowledge will have their own fair opinions, and there is no need for me to repeat them. Furthermore, the author is not an expert and has only observed a few things, so I dare not make hasty remarks for fear of being ridiculed by experts. However, for more than ten years, I have seen that the so-called promotion of physical education by the school authorities and the main physical education administrators in general universities and middle schools have made inappropriate arrangements and entered into dangerous detours, which not only harm young people at the time, but also endanger the foundation of the country and ruin the nation. If this continues, the consequences will be unimaginable. Now that the Ministry of Education is about to convene a national sports conference, there will be many reforms in school physical education. I am not talented, but I dare to present my usual observations and what the school authorities and main physical education administrators in general universities and middle schools have done wrong in the past and what urgently needs to be changed in the future, in order to provide some humble opinions before the national expert conference. I hope that any omissions will be corrected.

(1) Lack of Teachers Often Occurs; the Government Should Establish Specialized Schools. Considering the number of schools nationwide, the allocation of physical education teachers, regardless of their quality or quantity, is inadequate. As a result, either the material is not suitable for the job or unqualified people are used to fill the positions, gradually leading to the current incoherent state of physical education. The school authorities do not see this. They only need to find a person with a false reputation and a title to serve as the main physical education administrator of a school. They do not care whether the arrangements are appropriate or whether the promotion is widespread. What they seek is only whether our school can win a certain championship or a certain prize, and they boast to the public that this is the development of physical education in our school, this is the appropriateness of our school's promotion. Alas! The authorities' misunderstanding of physical education is like this, and the physical education administrators' facilities and arrangements are like that. It is appropriate that a young athlete suddenly leaps to become the director of physical education at a university. Football masters and basketball stars can almost all be filled as physical education professors in universities and middle schools. Alas, it is difficult to hope that the promotion of current school physical education can be done in this way. Considering the situation, the problem does not lie with the athletes or general star athletes, but with the government's inability to establish more specialized physical education schools to cultivate talent and distribute them throughout the country. The school authorities' pursuit of false reputations and lack of practical promotion is also an inexcusable thing.

(2) Economic Resources Must Be Appropriately Allocated and Managed. Some school authorities view physical education as a tool to flaunt, while others view it as a burden. The former causes the creation of a special class of school athletes, while the latter fosters a generation of weak and self-admiring young men. Looking at schools across the country, there are many that do not hire physical education teachers, do not make physical education a compulsory subject, and have no sports grounds or physical education equipment. The only excuse given by the authorities is that they are affected by the economy, and they do not consider the relationship between academic work and physical health, or the future of young people and the nation. It is so sad to talk about school education in this way. I hope that in the future, school authorities, no matter what kind of difficult environment they are in, will strive to eliminate this problem, determine the funds for school physical education, promote physical education, cultivate the nation's vitality, and lay a century-long foundation for the country. Then it will be fortunate. However, there are also those who say that it is inappropriate for those who do not contribute a penny to the promotion of physical education, and it is also inappropriate to misuse large sums of money on athletic schools. There are many universities and middle schools that use superficial methods of promotion, collecting annual physical education fees from all students and spending them on a small number of athletes, while neglecting the majority of students. This kind of special training for athletes, using the price paid by the majority of people to benefit a small number of people, is actually a dangerous step in promoting physical education. It is especially important for those in charge of school physical education to reflect and improve on the occurrence of this kind of abuse. If it is said that schools should promote physical education, they should have adequate funding, but the allocation must be equal and appropriate, and it must be consistent with the principle of taking from the public and using it for the public.

The Past and Present of the World Games (13)

(12) A Glimpse of the Venue of This Year's Games

Among all the buildings in the Olympic Village, the most outstanding is the Olympic Village itself. It used to be a desolate and shabby area, but now it has become a glorious and magnificent sports village. The main entrance and the general office of the venue are purely Spanish-style buildings, and the surrounding stands and dining halls are designated for each country to avoid mixing.

The Olympic Village is exclusively for athletes and staff from various countries to reside in, and can accommodate two to three thousand people. The village is located west of Los Angeles, overlooking the Pacific Ocean, and is conveniently located between sixteen competition venues and training grounds. The houses in the village have two rooms each, accommodating four people. There is also a management office and a dining hall. The dining hall is about 1,200 feet long and divided into several rooms, so that each country's team can bring their own chefs and prepare their own food and drinks. The construction cost was as high as 500,000 US dollars. As for the female athletes and female coaches, they live in the dormitories of the University of Southern California, which are very close to the venue.

The Olympic Stadium The Olympic Stadium is located in the Olympic Park and includes a track and field stadium, boxing arena, wrestling arena, and art museum. Its construction was planned ten years ago, and it is located near Los Angeles, with extremely convenient transportation. The track and field stadium can accommodate 105,000 people. The track is one mile in circumference and 220 meters straight. There are locker rooms for thousands of people. The construction began in 1921, and it was first opened in 1923, accommodating 80,000 spectators at that time. Three years ago, someone contracted to expand it for one million US dollars.

Swimming Pool The pool is connected to the track and field field. It is 50 meters long and 20 meters wide. One end is 1.5 meters deep and the other end is 5 meters deep. The water is extremely clean. The stands are made of very strong cement and can accommodate 10,000 people. Underneath the stands are locker rooms, bathrooms, offices, etc. The construction cost was as high as 250,000 US dollars.

Fencing Room This is the gymnasium of the California military camp. The building is also very strong, with a high roof and lush wisteria, which is quite spectacular. The floor is 90 meters long and 45 meters wide, suitable for eight fencing competitions. The surrounding area can also accommodate 10,000 spectators, with entertainment rooms, locker rooms, and offices.

Art Museum The art performances are held in the Olympic Stadium, which has nineteen exhibition rooms, adjacent to the fencing arena. The surrounding area is shaded by trees and the flowers are competing for beauty, making it a perfect place for art competitions.

Boxing and Wrestling Boxing, wrestling, and weightlifting are held in the Olympic Stadium, which can accommodate 10,000 spectators. The location is in the center of the Olympic Park.

Velodrome The construction cost was as high as 500,000 US dollars. It is constructed entirely of sturdy wood, forming a sloping, semi-concave shape. It was designed and built by the International Cycling Association and can accommodate 85,000 spectators. The construction cost was 250,000.

Rowing and Sailing The rowing venue is at the Marine McLaines Stadium. In addition to the docks, referees' seats, and offices, there are stands that can accommodate 15,000 people. The river is 2,000 meters long and 130 meters wide. Both banks of the river can accommodate 100,000 spectators. The Los Angeles seashore sailing competition venue can accommodate tens of thousands of spectators. In addition, the polo field and golf field are flat and wide, also serving as part of the Olympic Games venue.

Free Talk

Blazing Grandiose Words

Old Man Jiu Gong, Ma Xiangbo

In my life, I have died three or four times (please refer to the immortal four of the old man Xiang in this column on May 22). I remember one time, at the age of four, I had smallpox. Even the small coffin was prepared, and the clothes for going into the coffin were all put on. My father had just returned from outside, and he hugged my body and wept loudly. I don't know how, but I suddenly heard my father's crying, and I suddenly woke up and said with sobs:

"I won't die, I want to make meritorious service before I die!"

At first glance, this sentence seems very despicable, but it is not. When I was young, I wanted to make meritorious service, but I had already realized that one must do something in this world, and there was no dream of getting promoted and making a fortune. This pure and good idea of being superior to others comes from religious upbringing. This religious upbringing was given by a religious family. Because I had a religious family and a religious environment, I heard religious principles every day, and my state of mind was great from a young age, and when I opened my mouth, I couldn't help but speak blazing grandiose words.

People say that religion is foolish. In fact, it may be crazy, but not necessarily foolish. Literati who love to drink must drink to the point of being very drunk, drunk to the point of being in a world of clouds and mist, like being crazy, before good poems can be written. Religious people have firm beliefs, so sincerity can move mountains and open rocks. To others, it seems foolish, but I consider myself crazy.

With a crazy belief, then one can become a religious person! Similarly, with a crazy belief, then one can become a scholar. In the world, I don't know how many scholars have succeeded after going crazy. I have a crazy belief in religion, so I also have a crazy interest in science. It is because of this that I have a special interest in science!

Records of a Gathering West of Shanghai

— Lu Jingqing

The Xuhui area west of Shanghai is lush with shade, especially suitable for summer scenery. The green fields are secluded and serene, the water and trees are clear and bright. Elegant companions share carriages, bringing wine and musical instruments, a truly delightful and pleasing experience. Li Yunlao from Jiaochuan recently returned from Jinzhou. Zhu Zhang Ziqiao has just returned from Jingyuan. They invited old friends to a gathering at Bai Mei’s residence (in the western suburbs of Xuhui). Xiong Fenghuang, Huang Bao-yi, Li Zushen, Yin Ruli, and other gentlemen also came to join the excursion. Carriages arrived one after another. Old and new friends, like wine stars and literary stars, gathered in high spirits, filling the room with the joy of spring. Their connected hems touching, fortuitously mirroring the mythical voyage to Penglai. Loosening their robes and leaning on the railings, they savored the magnificent scenery. The midday sun cast cool shadows, and the gentle breeze dispelled the heat. Gazing afar at the Brahma Ferry and Hongjing, the verdant beauty resembled a painting. The ancient Longhua Pagoda seemed to stretch its neck to peer at us. The surrounding emerald green hues filled the view like a red gauze window. Soon, the food and wine were abundant, knives and forks clattered, delicacies piled high, and fragrant wine was poured. They discussed profound and refined topics, feeling relaxed and joyful. They contemplated matters of the nation and family, debated ancient and modern times, expressing their pure and untainted thoughts and lofty aspirations. The long night was filled with feasting and merriment. Adding to the atmosphere were blooming branches, enhancing the colors of the wine vessels. Piles of snowy white fruit tasted as sweet as jade nectar. Late cabbages and early chives offered the refreshing flavors of home. Fragrant lychees and sweet apples, mountain delicacies piled high. Purple eggplants and green beans added to the pleasant flavors. Vegetarian duck and gluten were cooked to perfection. The flavors were rich and satisfying, truly delightful. The cook, Yunlao, usually a Buddhist, is known for his skill with vegetarian cuisine. He modestly calls himself old and clumsy, but he is a master of culinary arts (Li's employed a renowned chef). Extravagance is not like He Yun, but precision is like Wei Qiu. Both fragrant and clean, emulating Mao’s heavenly kitchen, carefully crafted and precise, following the family precepts of Bo Lu. Therefore, the guests were loath to leave, with some drinking too much. The dishes and wine on this day were prepared by the vegetarian restaurant "Caigengxiang" at Yunlao's request. The chef, Yang, once received (monthly) poetry-worthy sums from Japanese to work on Sakura Island, gaining fame. Recently returning to his home country, he now helms the kitchen, lauded as a culinary genius. Among the delicacies served were date paste silver ear fungus, "Seven Treasures Ambrosia," emerald green porridge, and fragrant snowy vegetables, which were particularly praised by the guests. Reminiscing on past friendships. Seemed the vegetables combined the best of fish. Who can say that vegetarian food is too simple, or that the flavor of Caigeng is bland?

Master Xiang sat among the guests, personally sharing his draft manuscripts on civil governance for everyone to peruse. People lauded his brilliant and insightful arguments, which he would devote himself to publishing. His fame would spread far and wide. Such literature is of utmost importance. Our cause is not solitary, and our hearts will endure forever. His transcendent ideas will be as popular and well-received as fine cuisine. After drinking a bit, Master Xiang's face was flushed, and he was slightly tipsy. The pink face reflected the snow. He enjoyed discussing metaphysics with a duster, forgetting the passing of time. His wonderful ideas continued to flow, like pearls rolling from his lips. Carried away by the revelry, he inadvertently slipped and fell. The venerable gentleman had lost his balance. Li Yunlao and Zhu Ziqiao had the appearance of brave soldiers. Yunhe and Zhuxia showed elegant demeanor. They wore homegrown straw hats with double tassels hanging down, full of ancient charm. Remembering the bleak state of the country, they were moved to tears of patriotism, perhaps to show their mature and patriotic intentions. Xiong Bingnian has been living a quiet life in Xiangshan in recent years, managing the children's welfare cause. His silver beard was like a lance, indicating his age. Like a cold pool and autumn moon, he had a clear and noble bearing. Since temporarily staying in Shanghai, he has been diligently involved with the Red Swastika Society. At his leisure, he showed his kindness and generosity, unparalleled in the world. As the banquet came to an end, he inscribed the words "Noble and Pure" on a small book of amateur writing and drawings as a gift. Master Zhu also graciously inscribed "Chest Filled with Five Mountains." Although only scraps of paper and broken silk, they are truly precious. When the honored guests departed, they ascended the platform together. Master Xiang, as if awakened from last night’s wine, also came with a cane. They took several photos together, leaving a lasting impression. This served as a memento of the elegant gathering, a sign that ancient pleasures would not be forgotten.

The Death of Luo Liangong

— Zheng Yimei

Luo Liangong, a famous scholar from Sichuan, passed away in his Shanghai residence a few days ago, much to the regret of those who heard the news. He had a large build and a light mustache, and was energetic in his conversations, speaking in a loud voice. He had the appearance of a long-lived person. Now, he suddenly passed away before reaching eighty, which was unexpected. In his younger years, he served in General Wu Luzhen’s military staff, devising strategies in the tent. The General deeply relied on him. The young General was handsome and charming, and prone to indulgence in pleasure. Luo Liangong strongly advised him against it, without flattering or pleasing his superior. The General also respected and avoided him for his uprightness and integrity, like Yan Ziling and Emperor Guangwu of Han. It could be said that without Luo Liangong, the General could not have achieved his high position, and without the General, Luo Liangong could not have fulfilled his own ideals. In his later years, Luo Liangong enjoyed reading classic texts. What he spoke of often had Zen-like wisdom. He also had an addiction to drinking, with an immense capacity. One day, a friend invited him to drink fifty-year-old aged wine. The aroma was strong and rich. Luo Liangong was overjoyed and drank several large cups. His friend tried to stop him, saying that aged wine should not be drunk in excess, as it could lead to a deep intoxication that is difficult to wake from. He suggested that a small taste would be better. Luo Liangong thought his friend was being stingy and did not listen. He drank several more cups, only stopping when he felt slightly tipsy. After the banquet, he said goodbye and returned home. It was during the dead of winter, and the biting wind assaulted his clothes, making him shiver with cold. He felt dizzy and almost fell. He struggled to keep his balance and hired a car to take him home. He fell ill for three days before recovering. He then believed that his friend's words were not meant to deceive him, and realized the harm of excessive drinking. After abstaining from alcohol for over a month, someone gifted him several bottles of Du's rose wine. He once again drank excessively. Luo Liangong was skilled in calligraphy. His works after drinking were even more inspired. His calligraphy of couplets could often be found in vegetarian restaurants in Shanghai. I knew Luo Liangong and admired his calligraphy. I kept putting off asking him for a piece. Now, I want to ask but it is impossible. It shows that things in this world are often lost due to procrastination, not just in trivial matters like requesting calligraphy. He was deeply devoted to his wife. Last year, his wife passed away from illness. He wept bitterly and became depressed from then on. His health gradually deteriorated. He fell ill this summer and died, likely due to his emotional distress. His funeral was very simple. His children are still young. I sincerely hope that colleagues in the art world can provide assistance.

Afterword to "The Talking Myna Bird" - Qian Xiaoshan

—

A myna bird that can speak anti-Japanese slogans is righteous. This reminds me of a poem about the Qin Jiliao bird in the collection of the Song Dynasty poet Lin Jishan. The note says: "In the south, people raise Qin Jiliao birds that can speak human language. A barbarian chieftain wanted to buy one for 100,000 coins. The owner, claiming poverty, said he would sell it. The Qin Jiliao bird said, 'I am a Han bird. I do not wish to enter barbarian lands.' It then stiffened and died." Today's myna bird can be compared to the Qin Jiliao bird, one after the other. I compose a poem to praise them:

The myna bird shouts anti-Japanese slogans frequently,

Some humans can't even compare.

Forever side-by-side with the Qin Jiliao,

A Han bird will never be a barbarian slave.

Casual Summer Chat

— Jixiang

A friend of mine once bought a pebble in Beijing. It was light red in color. At first glance, it looked no different from any other stone. But when placed in water, eight crab legs appeared in the water. The legs seemed to emerge from the stone, like a real crab. But taking it out to look at it again, it was still just a stone. No one could figure out where the leg shadows came from. It was truly strange. My friend also said that someone else got a stone that had a beauty inside, holding a pipa, with graceful manner. It appeared only vaguely. It was truly the work of gods. The value was more than the city's walls.

My family has a carved bamboo cylinder. The diameter is about three inches and the height is five inches. Over ten human figures are carved on it. All are hollowed out. Each person's face, movements, and expressions are vividly portrayed, as if they were alive. I don't know where it came from, but it is also a precious object.

A certain Tongcheng School writer of the late Qing Dynasty liked to judge the merits of contemporary writers with his students. When it came to inferior works, he would always say, "The writing is good, but alas, it's like hearing drums on a high mountain." The students didn't understand what he meant, so they asked. He said, "Hearing drums on a high mountain, the sound is not clear." The students all smiled wryly.

Recently, I saw Mr. Xiong Bing-san's self-written "Niannujiao" lyrics in a certain place, which read: "The setting sun reflects the twin peaks, watching the buildings compete to rise. Thousands of doors and households. Sigh, the people of southeastern China are exhausted. The lake and mountains are still full of songs and dances. Listening far away to the river tide, the Xutao roars, all to sue private enemies. Only the solitary cypress remains upright, its loyal spirit lasting for thousands of years. Remember the ministers of King Goujian, sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall, enduring hardship for the whole territory. An unparalleled beauty can help the country, shaming countless men. The enemy's strength is growing. Court disputes have not stopped. I see Jin soldiers crossing again. Where is the soul of the nation? Who will rule this land?" It was written while traveling in West Lake. His concern for the country and his family overflowed in the lyrics.

Modern Woman

— Moyi

— Shanghai Portrait Eulogies No. 2 —

I unintentionally obtained a woman’s diary fragment from Yun, who is known as a socialite. Yun wrote these six words on it: “Modern Woman’s Diary.” I don’t understand what Yun meant. I am copying it here so everyone can judge the reasoning:

“I made an appointment with Little Wang yesterday to come to my house at 2 PM today to go see a movie together. Who knew I’d waited until 2:30 and Little Wang still hasn’t arrived. I’m really angry! Little Wang doesn’t have money to pay for me to see a movie. Actually, I could pay for Little Wang too. There’s no need not to come, ah! Hmph, if it weren’t for Little Wang’s pretty face, I’m afraid no one would want this poor kid, right?

“At 2:45, I really couldn’t stand it anymore. I was just about to change clothes to go find Little Wang when Old Chen came, unexpectedly. If a person’s name has ‘Old’ in it, even a blind person would know that person’s appearance must be very old and ugly. But Old Chen has money. In this era, we young women need certain things. Beautiful young men are certainly indispensable, but it’s a pity they’re mostly poor. So, we might as well have one or two rich men with beards, so we can avoid economic panic. That’s what I mean by my attitude toward Little Wang and Old Chen. Now that Old Chen has come, even though I dislike him a little, I can’t treat him coldly. He said he came especially to invite me to go see a movie. I pretended to be very happy and agreed to his request.

“I hid all my stunning new clothes and only wore something unfashionable. I deliberately looked in the dressing mirror again and again. I frowned for a while, then sighed. He urged me to hurry. I said the clothes were too plain and dull, so I wasn’t going. Then he said, ‘Well then, let’s go cut some fabric first.’ Of course, I was extremely happy inside, but my face still maintained a displeased expression. I got into his big Buick car and went to Wing On Company. I picked out expensive fabric and cut more than three hundred dollars’ worth. He was still smiling, and the ash from the cigar in his mouth didn’t fall off. He didn’t care at all.

“At this time, there was a woman with a diamond ring on her finger who was also cutting fabric. I stared greedily at her diamond ring. Old Chen is really clever, really smart. He guessed what I was thinking and said to me with a smile, ‘Man, let’s go buy one too.’ I didn’t say anything, just gave him a very charming smile. We went to the Ulivon Foreign Firm again. I don’t know how many carats this diamond ring was, but anyway, it was very expensive. When Old Chen signed that check for thirteen hundred dollars, his fingers didn’t tremble at all.

“After we finished watching ‘Circus Flower’ at the Cathay Theatre, we went to the Li Dao Restaurant for dinner together. I was afraid that Little Wang was waiting for me at home, so I ate a little and then said I had a headache and wanted to go home to sleep. He took me home in his car. On the way, he put his arm around my waist and wanted to kiss me. As I struggled to refuse, my right hand touched a package of fabric, and the light from the diamond ring on my left hand shone into my eyes. So I didn’t refuse anymore. He bought a kiss for more than sixteen hundred dollars…”

Talking about Fujian Meat Floss

— A Jie

Yesterday, Mr. Bi Cheng wrote "A Narrative of the Origin of Meat Floss" in Ziyoutan, saying that meat floss was founded by Ni Hongshun in Taicang. Now, although the Shanghai Concession is vast, the sellers of meat floss still use the old brand of Ni Hongshun, just like the sauce duck and sauce meat of Lao Sanzhen Lu Gaojian. Without this brand, it is not enough to show the high quality of the product. It is also said that the method of making meat floss has a special secret. It is said that snake oil must be used to prevent spoilage and allow it to be stored in containers without removing the air, the same as canned food today. As far as I know, meat floss is produced everywhere, but the best is made in Fuzhou. Today, the most popular meat floss in Shanghai is the Dingri You meat floss from Fuzhou. I have never heard of Ni Hongshun from Taicang being so famous. Fujian meat floss is light, fluffy, and fresh. It melts in your mouth. It is red and oily, and its deliciousness is unmatched. It is a perfect snack with wine. If you eat it with Shaobing, it has a unique flavor. Six or seven years ago, "Sai You Tian," a shop set up by Fujianese people on Route Edward VII, began selling Dingri You meat floss from Fujian. Each jar cost one yuan and two jiao, which was two-tenths higher than the price in Fujian. There are many rich people in Shanghai, who didn’t care about the high price at first. Therefore, the business was booming and there was a shortage of supply. Now, there are many consignment shops everywhere. However, it is not easy to see the real Dingri You product, and the price has also gradually decreased. In fact, the characteristic of Fuzhou meat floss is that it has more pork fat added during the production, which makes it more flavorful and oily. To say that it is made with snake oil to avoid removing the air is a fabrication. Regardless of the difficulty of obtaining snake oil, even if it were available, how could it have preservative properties? It is not credible.

Random Thoughts

— Liusha

Miss! I sincerely advise you, don't keep lamenting the ugliness of your face in the mirror, and don't hate your stupidity. Your ugliness and stupidity, alas, will be your happiness. Miss! Do you know the golden beetle? How free it is to eat dewdrops in the grass! But when people discover that it has a golden shell, it is arrested and played with. This arrest, alas, shows that people love it. Similarly, people who love roses will break them off. Beauty! Love! Forget it.

The difference between a mistress and a maid is that the mistress is a little lazier, and the maid is more diligent. But in this society, laziness is a virtue, and the lazier you are, the more respected you will be.

A small clerk in a certain agency shows off his power to a primary school teacher with such force that he almost crushes the thin man to death. The reason is simply that he receives twenty more dollars of salary each month.

A certain high official of the Legislative Yuan in the current era, wearing a long mandarin jacket past his knees, with several pieces of Han jade around his waist, his demeanor is different from others. One day, he instructed his young attendant: "You can't become an official without smoking opium."

Have a big attitude, don't be too eager to seek things, don't visit before people visit you, without attitude there is no respect, if you're too eager to seek things you won't succeed, visiting before people visit you lowers your status - this is what a teacher taught me about dealing with the world, is it true?

Commercial News

Fluctuations in Gold Standard are Strong

Yesterday, the fluctuations in the gold standard were extremely drastic. The price was constantly rising and falling around 750 taels, with a total market swing of 7.5 taels. Later, it rose more than 4 taels. However, as the silver price suddenly reported a fall the previous night, the opening was high. Subsequently, news came of the United States issuing public bonds to aid finance. Upon hearing this news, the market became fervently bearish and immediately dropped. It fell from 51.80 taels to 44.30 taels. The exchange rate rose and then fell back. In the afternoon, it turned flat. Towards the end, it was within 50 taels, and people were inevitably anxious. In August, Yufeng Yong liquidated 385 bars, while short positions such as Hengxing and Hengyu increased their holdings. The short positions still paid 2-3 taels, with the minimum being 1.90 taels. However, there were still about 10,000 bars that had not been liquidated. The situation of the past day is recorded as follows:

The high opening was 750 taels. The September futures opened high at 750 taels, up 4.90 taels. The major firms unexpectedly fell by 3/16 to 1/8, and the silver price also fell by a small 1/8. As a result, buyers were active. Yuanmao Yong, Hongkang Yong, Hengxing and others took the lead in making deals, and the price rose from 49.50 taels to 51 taels. Afterwards, Tong Taichang, Hengxing, Hengyu, Yuanda Yongyuan, Taidadecheng and others sold, immediately falling by 3 taels. Almost at the same time, the bonus bank mutual fund made 6875. Citibank also sold 30 yuan in October, reaching 47.70 taels at 9:20. In an instant, the price rose by 4 taels, because Dadecheng, Fushun Shunli, Hengyu Yifeng and others competed to buy. HSBC also bought 75 August US dollars, pushing the price up to 51.80 taels. HSBC's listed prices did not change, and then returned to 49.5 taels, with Tong Taichang and others selling. Subsequently, there was a rise and fall of 1 tael or so. Near 10 o'clock, it increased to 50.5 taels. However, after learning that the United States would issue public bonds to help the market, people's minds were fickle and the price was not supported. It dropped 5-6 taels at a time. However, from 10:15 to 10:45, there was still a gyration of 1 tael or so. Hengxing Yifeng, Yongzhifeng, Yongfutai, Hengyuan, Taifuyu, Qianchangxiang, Daxingyong and others successively sold, with the September US dollar settlement at 30 yuan. Until 11 o'clock, it finally reached 44.30 taels, and then turned flat. It was heard that a certain bank bought 105 current bars, and also 420 bars, at a price of 46 taels, sold by Runchangyu. Moreover, Yuanheng Hengyu and hedging came to buy, so the price was pulled up by 3 taels to 47.40 taels. Hengxing came out again, and at 11:30 it was 45.80 taels. At that time, it rose again by 1 tael, reaching 7.1 taels. When the midday closed at 46.60 taels, it fell again by a small 5-6 qian.

The afternoon market was soft and then hardened. The afternoon market opened softly at 45.80 taels and immediately went upward. Because Zhaofeng Chang, Yuanmao Yong, Hengchang Yong, Daxing Yong and Hengyu all entered, it was heard that speculators also bought in, because the exchange market was easier to improve. No Major Changes in Silver Dollar Market

The market situation remains sluggish as yesterday was Monday, and banks were open. Under normal circumstances, silver dollar transactions would be more frequent. However, it is currently the hot summer season, and buyers and sellers are not as active as usual. Therefore, the market lacks competitive heat, and prices have not changed much. The premium remains stable, with only a difference of 0.25. The silver market appears stable on the surface, but the underlying liquidity seems slightly tight. There is a relative shortage of "huatou touchen" (premium notes), but fortunately, banks had mortgage loans available the day before, otherwise, there might have been cause for concern.

Premium Rates Unchanged in Morning and Afternoon: "Foreign Premium" opened slightly better in the morning market, up 0.2 hao from the previous afternoon, at 6 qian 9 fen 5 li 2 hao and a half. The afternoon market saw balanced supply and demand, so the price remained unchanged, the same as the morning market. "Silver Premium" was 1 qian 4 fen in both the morning and afternoon markets, slightly better by 1 fen from the previous afternoon. "Huatou jia shui" (premium notes with added water) surprisingly reached 2 qian 5 or 6 fen, with banks quoting 6 fen.

Supplement of Shen Bao

Candidates Passing Higher Civil Service Exam Intend to Voluntarily Withdraw Qualifications

— Foshi

Last year's Higher Civil Service Examination was marked by exceptionally grand ceremonies. The expenditure alone was said to have reached over a million, truly befitting a major national talent selection event.

According to a Beijing dispatch yesterday, "The candidates who passed the previous Higher Civil Service Examination are scheduled to hold an annual meeting on August 6th, intending to request the National Government to strictly implement the appointment of qualified candidates after passing the examination. Otherwise, all personnel will return their certificates to the Examination Yuan and voluntarily withdraw their qualifications." Based on this, it seems that none of the gentlemen who passed the Higher Civil Service Examination have been appointed, so they are now anxious and want to voluntarily withdraw their qualifications. In reality, this may not be necessary, because based on the titles of these gentlemen, the country spent over a million dollars and held a grand examination ceremony, which is not easily obtained, and should be satisfied and forgiving.

Originally, "Don't become an official unless you have someone in court" has always been a golden rule. If you have strong backing, you will naturally become an official even if you are not qualified. Conversely, no matter what qualifications you have, it is useless. So, when the Higher Civil Service Examination was held, I predicted it was a waste of effort, because the gentlemen who went to take the Higher Civil Service Examination must not have any behind-the-scenes support. If you had support, you would have already become an official and be content, and would not be willing to take the exam again. So I know that even if you are admitted, it will still be useless. This is a certain truth.

The country's selection of talent is just a façade. Please carefully calculate how many first-class important figures there are in the current government (not counting those out of office), how many second-class important figures, how many third and fourth-class important figures, and how many relatives and friends of these important figures. How many rice bowls are there in total? How can it be the turn of the gentlemen who only have qualifications and no power? The Higher Civil Service Examination has already been taken, and you have already obtained your qualifications, so the country has fulfilled its obligations regarding the examination. What else can be said?

Furthermore, assuming you have a strong backstage boss, it is better to become an official. Even if you mess up, you can get away with it. If you don't have a reliable backstage boss, even if you become an official, you will not be able to stay in your position peacefully. Even if you are appointed with great difficulty, it will only be a few days or months of official luck. I guarantee you will step down, and there will be no hope of a rapid rise.

However, not all backstage bosses are the same. It is best to have some connection with the family, as it will have unexpected effects. Other relatives are secondary, and friends are even less important. If you want to become an official, you should think about how to establish some family relationship with the most important figures. This is originally a shortcut to success. Don't take qualifications to heart.

Science

Insecticide, Disinfectant, and Preservative

— Dream

Summer diseases are half transmitted by lice and insects, and half caused by carelessness in handling food. If effective and economical medicines can be used artificially to kill insects, and appropriate disinfection and preservation measures are applied to food, microorganisms will have no chance to develop, and the source of disease will be cut off. Here are some of the most common preservatives and insecticides, which are also part of household hygiene.

Carbolic Acid: Carbolic acid solution is an extremely effective insecticide. However, it is extremely poisonous and should not be ingested or come into contact with the eyes. It is very effective for removing lice or as a disinfectant for non-food items. It is available in all pharmacies, but it is quite complicated to make it yourself.

Sulfur: Sulfur is a good insecticide, especially for bedbugs. Sprinkling sulfur powder or applying a paste of sulfur and water inside bed frames or palm fiber mattresses can eliminate bedbugs. For full room disinfection, burn sulfur in the room to create sulfur dioxide. If the air in the room is dry, it is very toxic to fleas, flies, and other pests, and can prevent insect eggs from hatching. However, it has very little effect on microorganisms. Therefore, it is best to spray a small amount of water to humidify the room air, which will increase its ability to kill bacteria at the same time. Generally, burning two to three pounds of sulfur in 1,000 cubic feet for 24 hours can completely kill bacteria. Therefore, it is best to use this type of disinfection in rooms where someone has died from an infectious disease.

Salicylic Acid: An effective preservative. Because it is non-toxic, it can be used to preserve food. Adding a small amount to food or paste (Western paste can be made with it) can prevent spoilage for a long time. It has a very strong ability to prevent the growth of bacteria. This substance is available in pharmacies and is very cheap (about 20 cents can be used 30-40 times). It is complicated and uneconomical to make it yourself.

Boric Acid: Everyone knows that boric acid water disinfects. It is also very cheap (usually used to wash eyes). Although its bactericidal power is relatively weak, its preservative power is very strong. Adding one part boric acid and one part borax to milk can prevent acidification. It is commonly used in foods such as butter and cheese.

Of the above four types, two are insecticides and disinfectants, and two are preservatives. There are few mosquitoes and flies in Shanghai, but bedbugs are a constant problem. They first appear in pine boards, and then spread throughout the room, making them difficult to control. Using the above-listed insecticides can quickly cure them. Food spoilage and unwanted fermentation can be avoided by using the above two types of preservatives. Adding a small amount of preservative to household cooking, milk, or yellow wine can prevent the growth of microorganisms and keep them fresh for a long time. The reporter has tested this in practice and achieved good results, so I dare to tell the readers.

End

The Life of Ah San in Hell

— Huanhua

In a corner of the alley, there is a different world. An Ah San gentleman has set his sights on this piece of land as a temporary dormitory. Two newspapers are spread on the ground as bedding. On one side of the wall, two nails are nailed, and a rope made of torn rags is tied to hold a three-foot cube of old burlap bag. It can be considered a blanket or a tent. If it is to be considered a tent, just lie down facing the wall and pull the burlap bag behind you, then the tent is fully established. Fortunately, there is a natural screen of a trash can at the head, and a high-end hatbox is placed at the foot, with an overpass building covering it. This place is weatherproof. In the eyes of Ah San, it looks like a magnificent and comfortable nest.

Mr. Ah San has nothing to do all day long. He lies in the tent and takes out his favorite smoking set, which is a short bamboo gun, a smoking lamp made of a Western candle head and a waste light bulb cover, and a wire needle. He puts the cigarette can into the teapot, where he smokes the red pill ash discarded by others, taking pleasure in his leisure. He sucks one puff after another, but unfortunately there is not much ash, so he has to suck it into the bowl and then dig it out of the bowl, digging and sucking again, repeating the process endlessly.

Page 16

When the tobacco craving is satisfied, he takes the rectangular tin box used for biscuits and begs for leftovers from the households in the alley. After a hearty meal, he sits on that special bed, takes off his short shirt with hundreds of holes in his hand, and issues an order to exterminate the lice that are as dense as pearls. He picks them out one by one and puts them into his mouth, like eating fried soybeans. From his smiling expression, you can see that he is enjoying himself.

Another Mr. Ah San, with a burlap bag full of oil stains on his upper body, wearing a pair of broken shoes of different sizes picked up from the garbage dump, and his hair is four or five inches long, forming cakes. He is holding a magnetic-eroded iron washbasin as his dining furniture. Every day at twelve o'clock, the hunger in his stomach naturally tells him that it is noon and that he should go to the paradise he goes to every day to wait for his god of food to descend.

He braves the wind and rain, using his two legs as a car, and rushes to the entrance of this alley. After a while, a waiter from a restaurant delivering meals comes out of a house in the alley with plates and bowls. He jumps forward like a child seeing a nanny, and pours all the leftovers that people have not finished eating into the washbasin. He sits on the steps of a cooler house and uses his five fingers as nimble chopsticks to enjoy slowly. He is determined not to give up until he has licked all the remaining juice in the basin.

Afterwards, he looks for two cigarette butts on the nearby ground to light and smoke to relieve his fullness. Sometimes, when he arrives at the entrance of the alley and sees that it is still early, he runs to the houses in the area opposite the alley in the human flesh market to ask for a few copper coins. As long as he stands at the door, the foul smell emanating from his body and the fragrance of the modern salted meat ladies fight each other, they will willingly take out money for him. He never fails to win.

Family Problems

Family Education

— Youru

"Good boy, don't cry! Listen, the 'Old Turtle' who sells cooked side dishes is here. I'll buy you five copper coins worth of beef to eat." When the mother couldn't stop her son from crying, she used this "promise" as a condition to stop her son from crying.

"Mom, the Old Turtle is here! Call him into the alley! Where's the money? Hurry up and give it to me, I'll buy it myself." The son urged his mother urgently to fulfill the verbal contract just now.

"Nonsense! Where would Mom get so much extra money to buy you snacks? If you want money, why don't you ask your dad? He dresses well, eats well, and even gambles and visits prostitutes. He doesn't care about his son at all! Yesterday, I was still telling him that Ah Bao's classmates go to the Great World every day, watch dog races, play in dance halls, and have a lot of fun. I asked him when he would learn to go out and play for a while, so that the child wouldn't be envious of others. Who knew he would pull a long face and ignore me!"

"Mom, why doesn't Dad pay attention to Mom?"

"Oh! Good son, how would you know about your dad's affairs? He's been fighting like fire with that 'dirty bitch' since he got her! With her, why would he care about your mom?"

"Mom, didn't you say that salted meat old man? I always see Dad and have to scold him to vent my anger for Mom!"

"Good son! My good son! What you said is right, that kind of father really deserves to be scolded! If you can be so filial to Mom, Mom will definitely buy you a pair of foreign new leather shoes. When your birthday comes, you can wear them to show off!"

Ladies and gentlemen! Please look at the story above. Isn't it often heard in Chinese families? Analyzing and commenting on such ordinary words, we can at least get the following meanings:

(1) There is no need to keep one's word, as long as it can deal with the present situation.

(2) Anyone old can be casually scolded as an "Old Turtle."

(3) Develop children's habits of eating unsanitary snacks and spending money recklessly.

(4) Enlighten children with knowledge of places such as game halls, dog racing tracks, and dance halls... and arouse their bad desires?

(5) Implant in children's minds the impressions of "gambling," "prostitution," "dirty bitches," and "salted meat"...

(6) Guide and encourage children to resist the reason of their elders.

(7) Leather shoes must be foreign-made, which can at least cultivate children's psychology of despising domestic products and valuing foreign goods.

(8) Children also study to celebrate their birthdays, and even teach him to show off. This is because they are afraid that he has no vanity, and they are actually encouraging and guiding him.

Alas! This is Chinese family education!

End

At a Dinner Party

— Yiping

He couldn't stand the cunning and deceitful machinations on the political stage, so he secretly returned from Nanjing. He thought that his actions were unbeknownst to anyone, but that evening he received a notice for a dinner party - after graduation, he and several like-minded classmates held a dinner party once a month. He suspected that their methods were so clever; so he changed his clothes, smiled slightly at the thin teenager in the mirror, and wished himself good luck in finding a job in Shanghai that suited his personality.

He followed the address on the notice and stepped into the Xinghualou Restaurant. Little Zhang seemed surprised, when did Maodun (because he admired Maodun) return?

It was still early, and only Little Zhang asked the waiter to move the orange rows of tables. The two old friends who had not seen each other for a long time briefly talked about what had happened since their separation. He asked how they knew he had returned to Shanghai?

"Where? The recent regulations of the association have not changed the address. No matter what, we send the notice at the end of each month."

In a flash, the guests were seated, and they expressed special welcome for his return. Because the association publishes a magazine, and he has the alias of Maodun, he naturally has a considerable understanding of literature and art.

After a few rounds of wine, the atmosphere at the table was unusually thick. Everyone's face showed a rare smile, and everyone forgot that their current lives were completely opposite to their hopes in school. The small restaurant was filled with the vitality of youth, just like the life a few years ago.

The direction of the conversation turned to his political life, because among the classmates present, he was the only one who had been on the political stage after graduation. He drank a glass of wine, a bitter smile appeared at the corner of his mouth, and said.

"The political stage is like a dyeing vat, where white materials change color; it is also like the old civilized drama, where cats jump and dogs bark." His fiery eyes stared at a certain point and continued, "Alas! If I were a woman, I would rather sell my body."

He was originally a skeptic, and his words were even more bizarre after returning from Nanjing. The classmates at the table of course knew his temperament, so they diverted the conversation to sound movies, dance halls, and other topics.

He asked about everyone's lives. They were either small clerks in a foreign company or teachers in a small school. He wanted to find a job in Shanghai that suited his personality, but it gave him another disappointment.

He sullenly drank wine and returned home. On the bank of the Dongxin Bridge, he heard a miserable cry, "Here it comes! Here it comes!" "Is it so difficult to sell one's body?" He said to himself, walking home with his long shadow, thinking of a maxim: "To eat, one must be corrupt! And cunning and deceit are the working steps of corruption!"

End

Stepping Out of School

— Yuxian

I vaguely remember a cooler long night, when a few friends chatted idly on the grass in the campus. The lamplight shone down through the scattered gaps in the trees, and we could still see a few shining faces. All future hopes were smiling contentedly at that moment. It was the night of the graduation ceremony. Six years of studying under the window had earned us a diploma, but once the classmates separated, the true feelings of reluctance prompted us to have one last dinner party. The scene of laughter and lively conversation at the dinner party, who knew that it would be replaced by the melancholy of today's memories!

In early summer, the weather was cool in the morning. A car was heading towards the railway station in the gentle breeze. Jun and Wei were my closest friends. I couldn't refuse their enthusiasm, and I was actually reluctant to part with the last moment of being together. They sent me to the station. The station seemed to have changed its atmosphere, suffocating us and making us unable to say a word. A gloomy and depressed mood of separation completely occupied everyone's hearts. Finally, in the miserable farewell of "keep in touch often," the train headed towards my hometown. I occupied a corner of the carriage, imagining their dejection when they returned to school, and I couldn't help but shed tears silently.

My hometown was gradually approaching. The station where we had parted on a snowy night six years ago showed a decorated smiling face in the sunlight to welcome me. The hometown accent that I hadn't heard for a long time was gradually mixing with the noise; in the crowd, an apple-like small face was raising its hand and shouting my name. That was my younger brother, Pingying, whom I hadn't seen for six years, and he had grown so tall.

The hometown in my dreams was realized in front of me. It was not as wonderful as I had dreamed. After a week, I really felt it. This was my first taste of the bitterness of life, and it was also something unexpected after stepping out of school.

The conflicts between family members cannot be searched out from the faces of others by those who have not experienced them themselves, and those who have suffered its hardships do not bother to tell others in detail, because even if they can get the sympathy of others, sympathy cannot help me. Now I am being squeezed out of my hometown by the four words "family conflict," but it does not include "marriage" or even smaller things.

I was back on the train that had sent me back to my hometown on a drifting journey. No one saw me off, and no one pitied me. The lack of true sympathy in mankind was exposed here, and a cup full of bitter wine was placed in front of everyone who had been abandoned.

Three days later, I found out about Jun and Wei's whereabouts. They had jointly opened a bookstore, and I was responsible for proofreading and writing some things. Life was also very peaceful. The three of us lived together on the upper floor of the editorial office. The three of us lived for life. We worked very seriously, although we often had to stay up past midnight before we could sleep peacefully, but both our body and mind were very comfortable. After a month, it was already the Mid-Autumn Festival, a time for family reunions.

On the cool terrace of the editorial office, we were drinking wine at what could hardly be called a banquet. The moonlight was of course very sacred, shining all over the world, but the joys and sorrows of the world could not be understood by the sacred moonlight.

"Why don't you go home?" I drank a glass of wine and asked with some feeling.

"What about you?"

"I can't go home even though I have one!" I couldn't help but laugh.

"I can't go home even though I have one;" Jun repeatedly chanted, while raising a glass of wine and drinking it all in one gulp.

"Friends!" Jun's voice became impassioned, "Friends who can't go home, join hands and drink this cup together!"

The moonlight peeked out from the dark clouds to watch us drink together. The atmosphere at the dinner table became thick again. We talked about Zhuo's circus, Ibsen's A Doll's House, love stories between friends, and then the mischievous life at school...

When the banquet was over, Jun solemnly said, "From now on, no one is allowed to shed a tear, or let down our courage."

We extended our life for half a year in an environment where we were not allowed to cry:

The bookstore was raided due to some suspicion. Jun and Wei fled, and I was only responsible for proofreading and was not in trouble.

After that, my life drifted aimlessly. During that time, I also returned home to plant bamboo and raise turtles, and repented in seclusion, but in the end, "home" could not belong to me.

Alas! Drifting! Drifting! The seventh and seventeenth nights.

(Main text) The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. Chen Baosheng v. Pan Junqing for a guarantee case. (Main text) The defendant shall pay the plaintiff five hundred and seventy-five yuan, plus legal interest at a rate of five percent per annum from the date the plaintiff fills out the form until the end of the execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Jiang Shiyong v. Jia A'mao for a deposit case. (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. Zhang Xueshi v. Zhuang Xingsun et al. for a land appeal case. (Main text) The appeal and the ancillary appeal are both dismissed. The costs of the appeal and the costs of the ancillary appeal shall be borne by the appellant and the appellee, respectively. Bao Maomao v. Jin Wansheng Bamboo Firm for a debt appeal case. (Main text) The original judgment is altered. The appellee's claim in the first instance is dismissed. The litigation costs of all instances shall be borne by the appellee. Lin Renzhao v. Ni Yaorong et al. for a compensation case. (Main text) This case is transferred to the Second Local Court of the Shanghai Special District for handling. Sun Xiangji v. Zhao Liansheng et al. for a loan case. (Main text) The defendant, Cao Yunqi, shall repay the plaintiff five hundred and twenty-five yuan and five jiao. Zhao Liansheng shall be responsible for repaying two hundred yuan if he is unable to do so. The defendant and the counterclaim are dismissed. The costs of the lawsuit and counterclaim are borne by the defendant. Xu Zhongming v. Zhu Zhushi for a compensation case. (Main text) The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff for a loss of ninety-one yuan. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. Three-fifths of the litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff, and two-fifths shall be borne by the defendant.
